IRiphabhuliki yaseNingizimu Afrika iyizwe elilodwa elibumbene elibuswa ngumbuso weningi elisekwe phezu kwezibopho ezilandelayo: 
Ilungelo lokuvota kwabobonke abantu abadala, uhlu lwabobonke abavoti, ukhetho njalo ngezikhathi ezimiswe ukuthi kubenokhetho ngazo kanye nohlelo lokubusa oluqhuba ngenqubo yentando yeningi oluvumela iqhaza lamaqembu ahlukahlukene ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuphenduleka, ukunakekelwa kwezidingo nokusebenzela obala kukahulumeni.

umthetho noma isenzo esingahambisani nawo akukho emthethweni, futhi imibandela ezibekwe nguMthethosisekelo kufanele ilandelwe.

OKhomishani okuphawulwe ngawo kwisigatshana angasebenzisa igunya lamandla akhe futhi enze imisebenzi kakhomishani kwizifundazwe zawo njengoba kubalulwe kumthetho kazwelonke. 
Uma lingahleli iPhalamende, ngesikhathi kumenyezelwa isimo sokuvikela izwe, uMongameli kumele abizele iPhalamende emhlanganweni oyisipesheli phakathi kwezinsuku eziyisikhombisa senziwe isimemezelo.

yiPhalamende phakathi kwezinsuku eziyisikhombisa ezenziwe. 
Ukuze kufezeke imigomo yokusebenzela obala nakuziphendulela kwamakomidi asePhalamende akhiwe okumelwe kuwo amaqembu ahlukahlukene kumele aqaphe ukwenza kwawo wonke amaziko okuphepha, ngendlela ebekwe ngumthetho kazwelonke noma yimitheshwana noma izinqumo zePhalamende.

Ukuphatha kwabezepolitiki

Isifunda ngasinye sinelungelo

Isahluko 11 
Ohulumeni bezifundazwe babhekene nokufuna abasebenzi, ukuqasha, ukukhushulwa ezikhundleni, ukushintshela kwenye indawo umsebenzi kanye nokuxosha amalungu abasebenzi bakahulumeni emahhovisi okuphatha ngaphansi kombandela wamazinga afanayo kulokho okumiselwe abasebenzi bakahulumeni.

Ukumiswa nokusebenza kwayo 
Amandla nokusebenza kwawo 
Uhlobo olubalulekile lweBhange lesizwe laseNingizimu Afrika ukuvikela intengo yemali ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukukhula komnotho okungantengantengi nokuqhubeka njalo eRephabhliki. 
Umbuso wendabuko olandela uhlelo lomthetho wamasiko ungasebenza kuphela ngokuhambisana nomthetho noma yimuphi kanye namasiko, kanye nanoma yiluphi ushintsho noma ukucishwa kwalomthetho noma amasiko. 
uMongameli ongalisusa ilungu esikhundleni ngezizathu zokungaziphathi kahle, zokungakwazi ukuwenza umsebenzi ngenxa yesimo esithile noma zokungawazi umsebenzi. 
futhi ubhekele 
izintela, amalevi noma ezinye izintelo ngaphandle kwentela yeholo, intela yempahla noma imisebenzi ekhokhelwayo, intelo yentengo, intela yomhlaba nezakhiwo noma intela yemikhiqizo yakwamanye amazwe; 
Imali ingakhishwa esikhwameni semali sikazwelonke kuphela  
kanye nokuthi kuhlongozweni maqondana nokubolekwa kwemali nezinye izinhlobo zesikweletu ezizokwandisa izikweletu zomphakathi onyakeni olandelayo. 
Izimali ezabiwe ngesifundazwe ziya kuhulumeni wendawo kuleso sifundazwe, njengoba kusho isigaba 214, ziyisikweletu esiqonde ngqo esikhwameni semali yesifundazwe. 
unelungelo lokuthola ingxenye egculisayo yemali eqoqwe ngokukazwelonke ukuze akwazi ukuhlinzekela izidingo zomphakathi nokwenza imisebenzi enikezelwe kuwona; 
izithunywa ezimile zesiGungu sikazwelonke sezifundazwe, zamalungu eKhabinethe, zosekela bongqongqoshe, zabaholi bendabuko kanye namalungu anoma yiziphi izigungu zabaholi bendabuko; 
izigaba imali esetshenziselwa zona ezisetshenziswa ngokufana ezincwadini zezimali zombuso; 
Isinqumo sokumisa ukudluliselwa kwemali esifundazweni singathathwa kuphela njengokusho kwesigatshana, ngenhla, futhi  
IKhomishana izimele futhi ilawulwa kuphela nguMthethosisekelo kanye nomthetho futhi kumele ingavuni muntu. 
Isifundazwe noma umasipala angaboleka izimali zokuhlangabezana ndleko ezingaveli njalo, zezinto ezizokwenza ukuthi umasipala akwazi ukuqhuba umsebenzi lowo noma zokuhlangabezana nezindleko ezijwayelekile ezisheshe zedlule ngokulandela imibandela efanele emiswe ngumthetho kazwelonke, 
Okuphathene nezimali jikelele 
amandla ezezimali kanye nokusebenza ngobunyoninco kwezifundazwe nawo masipala; 
futhi ungathola ezinye izabelo zemali zikahulumeni kazwelonke ezinemibandela noma ezingenamibandela. 
futhi izintela ezingaquki ezibalwe ngokulinganisa intela engaqoqwa kunoma yisiphi isigaba sentela, samalevi noma sezinhlobonhlobo zentela ebekwe ngumthetho kazwelonke ngaphandle kwezimali zezintela ezivela ezinzuzweni zohwebo, kwintela yohwebo, intela yomhlaba nezakhiwo, noma izintela zemikhiqizo evela kwamanye amazwe. 
izibopho zezifundazwe nawomasipala njengokubeka komthetho kazwelonke; 
KuneKhomishana yezimali nokusetshenziswa kwezimali yeRephabhliki eyenza izincomo ezilindelwe kulesi sahluko, noma emthethweni kazwelonke, izethule kwiPhalamende, kwizishayamthetho zezifundazwe kanye nakunoma ngumthetho kazwelonke. 
Akukho lutho kulesi sigaba okuvimbela ukwabelana ngemali engenile yombuso ngokumaqondana nalesi sigaba phakathi komasipala labo abanamandla phezu kwesikhwama sombuso kanye nemisebenzi kuleyo ndawo. 
ukwehlukaniswa ngendlela egculisayo kwezimali eziqoqelwe esikhwameni sikazwelonke, zehlukaniselwa imikhakha kahulumeni kazwelonke, yezifundazwe neyezindawo; 
Uma izingxenye zikahulumeni zifuna ukuthenga impahla noma ubuciko bokwenza imisebenzi ethile, 
Ukumiswa 
Amandla kamasipala okuhlawulisa izintela empahleni yabantu, nezinye izintela zokukhiqiza nezemisebenzi eyenziwe noma egameni likamasipala, noma ezinye izintela, amalevi noma izintela zemikhiqizo evela kwamanye amazwe  
Minyaka yonke uhulumeni ngamunye kufanele ashicilele umbiko ngeziqinisekiso azinikile. 
Isikhwama semali sikazwelonke 
izinhlelo zokusetshenziswa kwezimali zikazwelonke zezifundazwe noma zendawo kufanele zethulwe nini; 
lingamisa ukudluliselwa kwemali engxenyeni kahulumeni kuphela ngesizathu sokuthi imigomo nezimiso ezibekwe kwisigatshana ngenhla zephulwe kabi kakhulu noma ngokuphindaphindwa. 
UMkhandlu sokuphatha sikazwelonke, sesifundazwe, umasipala noma yisiphi esinye isiphathimandla singaphoqelela umthetho kazwelonke oshiwo esigatshaneni, ngenhla, kuphela emuva kokubhekelela noma yisiphi isincomo esenziwe yiKhomishana emiswe njengoba kushiwo kwisigatshana, ngenhla. 
noma yiziphi izimiso okufanele zenziwe maqondana nesikweletu sezwe kanye neminye imibandela kazwelonke; 
kanye nezinga elingeke leqiwe lamaholo, izibonelelo nezinzuzo zamalungu ezishayamthetho zezifundazwe, amalungu eziGungu zokuphatha zomasipala zezigaba ezahlukene. 
Izinkantolo kufanele zisebenzise imithetho yamasiko uma lowo mthetho kuyiwona okufanele usebenze kodwa kuphela uma kuhambisana noMthethosisekelo kanye nanoma yimuphi umthetho ophathelene ngqo nomthetho wamasiko. 
ubungako besikhwama sombuso sikamasipala ngamunye; 
Ukuhlelwa kokusetshenziswa kwemali emkhakheni kazwelonke, wesifundazwe kanye nowendawo 
Kunesikhwama semali sikazwelonke okufakwa kusona yonke imali kanye nemali etholwe nguhulumeni kazwelonke, okufanele ikhokhwe, ngaphandle kwemali ekhishelwe ngaphandle komthetho wePhalamende. 
Isahluko 12 
Umthetho kazwelonke kufanele umise izinhlaka zokunquma amaholo, izibonelelo nezinzuzo zamajaji, zoMvikeli woMphakathi, zoMcubunguli omkhulu wamabhuku ezimali zikahulumeni 
Ukulawulwa kokugcinwa kwezimali 
Izindaba eziphathelene nezimali zesifundazwe nezendawo 
USihlalo kanye nesekela likasihlalo abangamalungu aphelele; 
Isigatshana asivimbeli ukusetshenziswa kwezimiso zokuthengwa kwempahla nobuciko bokwenza imisebenzi ezibekwe yingxenye kahulumeni ezihlinzekela okulandelayo: 
zingabolekwa kuphela uma kunesidingo sokuvala isikhala esikhathini sonyaka wezimali; 
angesetshenziswa ngendlela engakhinyabeza kakhulu futhi ngendlela engafanele imigomo kazwelonke yezomnotho, izinyathelo eziphathelene nomnotho ezeqe imingcele yezifundazwe noma ukuhwebelana ngokukazwelonke ngempahla, amasevisi, izimali noma imisebenzi; 
isidingo sokuqinisekisa ukuthi omasipala banamandla okufeza izidingo ezisemqoka zabantu okulindelwe ukuthi zifezwe ngumasipala futhi benze imisebenzi eyabelwe kubona; 
futhi isifundazwe kufanele sinikwe ithuba lokuziphendulela kuloko esithweswe icala ngako sibeke udaba lwaso phambi kwekomidi. 
Amandla esifundazwe okubeka izintela, amalevi ezinye izimali ezingena esikhwameni semali sikahulumeni ngezinkokhelo ezahlukile, noma ngezimali ezikhokhelwa izidingo zomphakathi  
Uhulumeni kazwelonke, wesifundazwe noma umasipala angaqinisekisa ukukhokhwa kwesikweletu kuphela uma isiqinisekiso sihambisana nemibandela ebekwe emthethweni kazwelonke. 
 izidingo zezwe; 
Ukuze ubhekelele izindaba eziphathelene nobuholi bendabuko, iqhaza abaholi bendabuko abangabanalo, umthetho wamasiko kanye namasiko emiphakathi elandela uhlelo lomthetho wamasiko  
ukulingana. 
kodwa umasipala akavunyelwe ukubeka intela yeholo, intela yokuhweba, intela yentengo ejwayelekile, intela yokusebenzisa izidingo zomphakathi noma izintela zemikhiqizo evela kwamanye amazwe. 
futhi kufanele alawulwe ngumthetho wePhalamende, ongashaywa kuphela emuva kokubhekelelwa kwezincomo yiKhomishana yezimali nokusetshenziswa kwezimali zikahulumeni. 
Imali ingakhishwa esikhwameni semali sesifundazwe kuphela  
Umthetho kazwelonke kufanele uhlinzekele uhlaka lokusetshenziswa kwezimiso ezishiwo kwisigatshana ngenhla. 
Umthetho wePhalamende kufanele umise uhlaka lokufinyelela ezinqumweni ngokulandelayo  
Izintela zesifundazwe 
IBhange lesizwe laseNingizimu Afrika liyibhange elikhulu laseRephabhliki futhi lilawula njengokusho komthetho wePhalamende. 
futhi izinhlelo zokusetshenziswa kwezimali kuyo yonke imikhakha kahulumeni kufanele ibonise ukuthi izimali zivelaphi nokuthi izimali okuhlongozwa ukuthi zisetshenziswe zizohambisana ngayiphi indlela nomthetho kazwelonke. 
Ikhomishana yezimali nokusetshenziswa kwezimali 
njengoba kushiwo ngumthetho wesifundazwe; 
noma yikuphi okunye ukwabiwa kwezimali okuya kohulumeni bezifundazwe nokamasipala, kuvela esabelweni semali sikazwelonke kanye nemibandela engabekelwa lokukwaba. 
Ingxenye yemali kazwelonke eya kwizifundazwe evela ezimalini zikazwelonke ingakhishwa ngqo esikhwameni semali kazwelonke. 
Isikhwama sezimali zesifundazwe 
ukudingeka kwezabelo zemali ezingaguqulwa kalula futhi ezilindelekile; 
Umthetho kazwelonke kufanele umise ikhomishani ezimele yokwenza izincomo maqondana namaholo, izibonelelo kanye nezinzuzo ezishiwo kwisigatshana . 
futhi ingalawulwa ngokomthetho kazwelonke. 
kodwa izimali ezibolekelwa izindleko ezijwayelekile ezisheshe zedlule  
Ngaphambi kokuthi iPhalamende lamukele noma livuselele isinqumo sokumisa ukudluliselwa kwezimali esifundazweni  
Uma omasipala ababili benamandla afanayo ngokwesikhwama sombuso kanye nemisebenzi emaqondana nendawo efanayo, ukwabiwa ngendlela efanele kwalawo mandla kanye nemisebenzi kumele kwenziwe ngokulandela umthetho kazwelonke. 
indlela efanele nenomphumela omuhle wokuhlawulisa izintela, amalevi kanye nemali ekhokhela imikhiqizo evela kwamanye amazwe angaphandle; 
nguMongameli, njengenhloko yokuphatha kazwelonke: 
Izinhlelo zokusetshenziswa kwezimali emkhakheni kahulumeni ngamunye kufanele zibonise  
Kunesikhwama sezimali zesifundazwe sesifundazwe ngasinye okufanele kufakwe kuso zonke izimali ezitholwe nguhulumeni wesifundazwe. 
kodwa kufanele kube nokubonisana phakathi kweBhange nelungu leKhabhinethe ebhekelele izindaba zezimali zikazwelonke. 
Umthetho kazwelonke oshiwo kwisigatshana ungashaywa kuphela emuva kokuthi kubhekelelwe noma yiziphi izincomo zeKhomishana yezimali nokusetshenziswa kwezimali. 
Iziqinisekiso zikahulumeni 
Lolu hlelo kufanele lwenziwe luqedwe phakathi kwezinsuku ezingu 30 senziwe isinqumo sehhovisi likazwelonke lokuphatha izimali. 
izinkambiso ezamukelwa njengezijwayelekile zokubika ngezimali; 
Ihhovisi likazwelonke lokuphathwa kwemali, ngokuvunyelwa njengelungu leKhabinethe elibhekele izindaba zezimali zikazwelonke, 
uhlelo lwezimali lukazwelonke, lwezifunda nolwezindawo lufanele lubenjani. 
amaholo, izibonelelo nezinzuzo zamalungu omkhandlu kazwelonke, 
Ingxenye yemali egculisayo yesifundazwe eqoqwe ngokukazwelonke kufanele idluliselwe kwisifundazwe ngokushesha futhi kungazange kubanjwe zimali kuyo, ngaphandle uma ukudluliswa kumiswe njengoba kusho isahluko 216. 
Umthetho kazwelonke noma wesifundazwe ungahlinzekela ukumiswa kwezindlu zabaholi bendabuko; 
Umthetho kazwelonke ungahlinzekela ukuthi ubuholi bendabuko, njengohlelo lokuphatha emkhakheni wezindawo, njengohlelo lokuphatha emkhakheni wezindawo, bube nesandla maqondana nezindaba ezithinta imiphakathi yezindawo. 
Umthetho kazwelonke kufanele umise ihhovisi likazwelonke futhi abeke izindlela zokuqinisekisa ukusebenza ngendlela esobala kanye nokulawulwa kokusetshenziswa kwezimali emkhakheni ngamunye kahulumeni, ngokuthi ethule  
Umthetho kazwelonke kufanele umise ukuthi  
Indawo engadlalwa ngabaholi bendabuko 
Uhulumeni wendawo nesifundazwe ngasinye  
Umasipala angabeka intela yempahla umuntu anayo, kanye nezintela zokukhiqiza, ngomsebenzi owenziwe egameni likamasipala; 
indlela egculisayo yokunquma ubungako bengxenye yemali etholwa yisifunda ngasinye; 
Umthetho kazwelonke ovezwe kulesi sigaba ungamiswa kuphela emva kokuthintana nohulumeni wendawo kanye nabeZimali neKhomishani yesikhwama sombuso, futhi uma sekucutshungulwe noma yisiphi isincomo sikaKhomishani. 
futhi kufanele asetshenziswe noma enziwe ngokulawulwa yimibandela ebekwe njengoba kusho lowo mthetho. 
izidingo nezinto ezibalulekile kuhulumeni kazwelonke, ezinqunyelwe emuva kokubhekelwa kwayo yonke imicabango efanele; 
Isifundazwe kufanele sizihlinzekele sona loko esikudingayo, njengoba kusho izimiso zomthethosisekelo waleso sifundazwe, ezingaphezulu kwezidingo ezilindelekile kumthethosisekelo. 
kufanele zikwenze lokhu ngendlela ehambisana nemithetho kazwelonke noma yesifundazwe emisa uhlelo olugculisayo, olulungile, olusobala, oluvumela ukuqhudelana futhi olusebenzisa imali ngendlela efanele. 
Ibhange elikhulu lesizwe 
isidingo sokuhlangabezan a nemigomongqangi ezwakalayo yokukhishwa kwentela; 
Isishayamthetho sesifundazwe singabeka  
IBhange lesizwe laseNingizimu Afrika, ngenhloso yokufeza izinjongo zayo, kufanele yenze imisebenzi yayo ngokuzimela kanye nokungabi nokwesaba, ukukhetha noma ukujivaza; 
Abaholi bendabuko

Izimali 
Amalungu asebenza kulezozikhundla njengoba kusho umthetho kazwelonke 
Inhlobo ebalulekile 
Amandla nemisebenzi yeBhange lesizwe laseNingizimu Afrika yileyo ejwayelekile kumabhange amakhulu, futhi okufanele imiswe emthethweni wePhalamende 
Ukwabiwa kungenziwa kuphela emva kokuqashelwa kwale ndlela elandelayo: 
noma njengokuhlinzeka koMthethosisekelo noma umthetho wePhalamende, omisa ukuthi imali ethile ibekelwe umsebenzi othile. 
ngokulinganayo, uhulumeni kazwelonke akaphoqwe yilutho ukuba anxephezelise izifundazwe noma omasipala abangaqoqi izimali ezilingana nezimali ezingaqoqwa noma izintela ezingakhokhwa. 
kanye nesidingo sokungaqinisi izintamo uma kubhekwana nezimo ezibucayi ezivelayo noma ezinye izidingo zesikhashana, kanye nezinye izimo ezinesisekela esifanayo. 
Ukuqokelwa esikhundleni nesikhathi sesikhundla samalungu 
amandla kanye nemisebenzi eyenziwa ngumasipala ngamunye; 
asivunyelwe ukumisa ukudluliswa kwemali isikhathi esingaphezulu kwezinsuku ezingu-120; 
izidingo zokuthuthukiswa nezinye izidingo zezifundazwe, zohulumeni bendawo kanye nawomasipala; 
Izigaba ezinconywayo ekwabiweni kwezivumelwano zokuthengwa kwempahla noma ubuciko bokwenza imisebenzi; 
futhi singaphoqelelwa khona kanjalo kodwa singasuswa kusekela esikhathini esedlule ngaphandle uma iPhalamende lisamukela lesi sinqumo emuva kokulandela uhlelo olusondelene nalolo olumiswe kwisigaba 76 
IKhomishana kufanele inikeze imibiko izikhathi ezijwayelekile ePhalamende nakwezishayamthetho zezifundazwe. 
angeke yenziwa ngendlela engalungile yokubandlulula inqubo yezomnotho kazwelonke, imisebenzi yezomnotho ngaphandle kokulandela imingcele kamasipala, noma ukuhanjiswa kwempahla kukazwelonke, imisebenzi, imali yebhizinisi noma yokusebenza; 
Ukuhlelwa kokusetshenziswa kwemali emkhakheni kazwelonke, wesifundazwe nowendawo kanye nako konke okuphathelene nokuhlela ukusetshenziswa kwezimali kufanele kugqugquzelele ukusebenzela obala, ukuphenduleka, kanye nokuphathwa kwezimali okunempumelelo emnothweni, nokuphathwa okunempumelelo kwesikweletu kanye nemisebenzi yomphakathi. 
Ngokumaqondana nesigatshana, kanye no, umasipala angahlawulisa  
Ukukhokhelwa kwabantu abasezikhundleni zikahulumeni 
IPhalamende lingasivuselela isinqumo sokumisa ukudluliselwa kwemali isikhathi esingeqile ezinsukwini ezingu-120 ngesikhathi, emva kokulandela uhlelo olubekwe njengokusho kwesigatshana . 
futhi ngokugunyazwa ngumthetho kazwelonke, angabeka ezinye izintela, amalevi noma ezinye izimali ezingena esikhwameni semali sikahulumeni ngezinkokhelo ezahlukahlukene, 
futhi Umthetho kazwelonke ungamisa uMkhandlu sabaholi bendabuko. 
ukwehluka kwezimo zomnotho phakathi kwesifundazwe ngasinye naphakathi kwezifundazwe ezahlukahlukile; 
UMthetho oshiwo kwisigatshana ungashaywa kuphela emva kokubonisana nohulumeni besifundazwe, ohulumeni bendawo abahlelekile kanye neKhomishana yezimali nokusetshenziswa kwezimali zikahulumeni, futhi kwabekelwa noma yisiphi isincomo sekhomishani; 
UMcubunguli omkhulu wamabhuku ezimali zikahulumeni kufanele anikeze iPhalamende umbiko; 
IPhalamende lingemukela umthetho oshiwo kwisigatshana kuphela emuva kokubhekelela noma yiziphi izincomo ezenziwe yikhomishana emiswe njengoba kushiwo kwisigatshana, ngenhla. 
Imali ebolekwe yisifundazwe 
futhi ukuvikelwa noma ukuthuthukiswa kwabantu noma izigaba zabantu abuyisele emuva ubandlululo olungalungile. 
kanye namalungu anoma iyiphi ikhomishana ehlinzekelwe kuMthethosisekelo, kubandakanya isiphathimandla sokusakaza esishiwo esigabeni 192. 
futhi lwamiswa yimitheshwana nezibopho zePhalamende. 
ISheduli 1 
sibophelela iRephabhliki ngaphandle kokwamukelwa nguMkhandlu kazwelonke noma uMkhandlu kaZwelonke sesifundazwe, kodwa kufanele sethulwe phambi komkhandlu kazwelonke kanye noMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe ngesikhathi esifanele. 
Umbala okake indawo eluhlaza okotshani, ngayinye iwububanzi obuyingxenye yokukodwa kokuhlanu yobubanzi befulegi. 
Isihloko esifushane kanye nokuqala ukusebenza 
Umuntu ongusihlalo emhlanganweni okusebenza kuwo leSheduli kufanele abize ukuba kuphakanyiswe emhlanganweni abantu abazomela ukhetho. 
Noma yisiphi isivumelwano samazwe ngamazwe siba yimithetho kwiRephabhliki uma singeniswe emthethweni ngokushaywa komthetho kazwelonke; 
Uma kuphakanyiswe abantu ababili kuphela, noma uma kusele ababili kuphela emva kwenqubo yokuchitha isetshenzisiwe, labo ababili benamavoti alingangayo,

futhi ngethembisa ngokuqinisekile ukuthi ngizokwenza imisebenzi yami njengelungu loMkhandlu kaZwelonke / njengesithunywa esimile kuMkhandlu kaZwelonke sezifundazwe /amalungu esishayamthetho sesifundazwe sase CD 
Isifungo noma isiqinisekiso sesekela likaMongameli 
Ukusetshenziswa komthetho wamazwe ngamazwe 
Yonke imisebenzi ebekwe ngokomthethosisekelo kufanele yenziwe ngokukhuthala futhi ngokungachithi sikhathi. 
Uma kuphakanyiswe ngaphezulu komuntu oyedwa - 
kufanele afunge noma aqinisekise ngaphambi kukaMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo. 
Ngaphandle uma kuhloswe ukuthi kwehluke, isimiso sikhuluma ngesikhathi sokuqala kokusebenza komthethosisekelo kusuke kushiwo isikhathi sokuqala ukusebenza kwaleso simiso. 
Ukumenyezelwa kwamagama abamele ukhetho 
zesiGungu kaZwelonke sezifundazwe kufanele afunge noma aqinisekise, phambi kukaMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo, noma elinye ijaji elijutshwe nguMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo, ngendlela elandelayo: 
ngawo wonke amandla enginawo. 
Ukuthuthukisa inqubo yentando yeningi evumela amaqembu ahlukahlukene ezombusazwe ukuba abambe iqhaza, imithetho kazwelonke kufanele ihlinzekele ukwesekwa ngezimali kwamaqembu epolitiki ameleleke ngokukazwelonke nakwizishayamthetho zesifundazwe indlela egculisayo nelandela ukumeleleka kwamaqembu. 
ISheduli 6 uhambelana nenguquko yohlelo yomthethosisekelo omusha osungulwe yilo mthethosisekelo, futhi nanoma yiluphi udaba olungavela mayelana naleyo nguquko. 
ngiyafunga / ngiqinisekisa ukuthi ngizokwethembeka kwiRiphabhuliki yeNingizimu Afrika futhi ngizothobela, ngihloniphe futhi ngiphakamise uMthethosisekelo kanye nayo yonke eminye imithetho yeRiphabhuliki; 
sisebenzisa amandla noma ukwenza umsebenzi omayelana nomthethosisekelo noma umthethosisekelo wesifundazwe; 
UMongameli angabeka izinsuku ezahlukene ngaphambi kwelanga elishiwo kwisigatshana , mayelana nokuhlinzekela ukusebenza kwezimiso ezehlukene ezishowo uMthethosisekelo. 
ukungadlulisi ngendlela eqondile noma ecashile noma yiluphi udaba oluyimfihlo engethenjwe ngalo; 
Imigqa ephakathi nendawo yale ndawo eluhlaza okotshani iqala ekhoneni elingenhla nelingezansi eduze kwesigxobo sefulegi, iyasondelana maphakathi nefulegi iqhubeke, owodwa eduze komunye ize iphelele phakathi nendawo kwicala elibhekene nalelo imigqa eqale kulona. 
ngizinikezela kwinhlalakahle yeRiphabhuliki nabo bonke abantu bayo. 
Isiphakamiso kufanele senziwe kwifomu elibekwe yimitheshwana eshiwo ku 9, ngezansi. 
UNdunankulu wesifundazwe, kanye nelungu ngalinye loMkhandlu sokuPhatha kwisiFundazwe, kufanele afunge/ aqinisekise phambi kukaMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo noma ijaji elijutshwe nguMongameli wenkantolo yoMthethosisekelo, ngendlela elandelayo: 
ilungu ngalinye elikhona, noma uma kungumhlangano woMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe, isifundazwe ngasinye esimelwe, emhlanganweni singavota ngevoti elilodwa; 
Uma kukhona ukungahambisani phakathi kwemibhalo eyahlukahlukene yomthethosisekelo, umbhalo weSingisi yiwona obusayo. 
Ifomu okwenziwe kulo lezi ziphakamiso kumele lisayinwe  
Ukuxoxiswana nokusayinwa kwezivumelwano zamazwe ngamazwe kungumsebenzi wesigungu sokuphatha sikazwelonke. 
ngizinikezela kwinhlalakahle yeRiphabhuliki nabo bonke abantu bayo. 
Uma kuphakanyiswe umuntu oyedwa, umuntu owengamele umhlangano kufanele amemezele ukuthi ukhethelwe esikhundleni. 
ngivikela futhi ngiqhubela phambili amalungelo abo bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika; 
futhi kuphindwe lokuvota uma kunesidingo kuze kucace ukuthi kuchithwa bani.

Ukuzimela

kufanele kuvotwe emhlanganweni ngevoti langasese; 
noma sisebenzisa amandla okusebenza emphakathini noma kwenziwa umsebenzi womphakathi mayelana nanoma yimuphi umthetho, kodwa kungafaki inkantolo noma isikhulu esibhekele umthetho;

kodwa lokhu akushiyi ngaphandle ukuniswa mayelana nalo mthethosisekelo womthetho obhekelekile kunoma yikuphi okuhlinzekelwe ngaphambi kwalolo suku.

UNgqongqoshe ngamunye kufanele afunge aqinisekise, phambi kukaMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo noma elinye ijaji elijutshwe nguMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo, ngendlela elandelayo: 
Isekela likaMongameli, kufanele lifunge noma liqinisekise phambi kukaMongameli weNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo ngendlela elandelayo: 
Isifungo noma isiqinisekiso sikaMongameli kanye nebamba likaMongameli 
Uma kuhunyushwa noma yimuphi umthetho, yonke inkantolo kufanele incamele noma yikuphi ukuhumusha okufanele okuhambisana nomthetho wamazwe ngamazwe kunokunye ukuhumusha okungahambisani nomthetho wamazwe ngamazwe.

ngiyafunga/ ngiyaqinisekisa ukuthi, njengejaji leNkantolo yoMthethosisekelo /lenkantolo eNkulu yokudluliselwa kwamacala / leNkantolo ePhakeme yase EF / leNkantolo yase GH 
Emhlanganweni okusebenza kuwo leSheduli, umuntu owengamele kufanele amemezele amagama alabo bantu abaphakamisiwe njengabamele ukhetho, kodwa angayivumeli inkulumompikiswano. 
Lenqubo kufanele iphindwe kuze kubenothola iningi lamavoti.

ngiyafunga /ngiyaqinisekisa ukuthi ngizokwethembeka kwiRiphabhuliki yaseNingizimu Afrika, futhi ngizothobela, ngilandele, ngiphakamise futhi ngigcine uMthethosisekelo nayo yonke eminye imithetho yaseRiphabhuliki;

ISheduli 3 
Izifungo neziqinisekiso 
Ngaphambi kwalolo suku noma yikuphi okuhambisanayo futhi ukuhlinzekela obekungabhekekile kumthethosisekelo weRephabliki yaseNingizimu Afrika, 1993, uzoqhubeka usetshenziswe. 
ngiyafunga/ ngiyaqinisekisa ukuthi ngizokwethembeka kwiRiphabhuliki yeNingizimu Afrika futhi ngizothobela, ngihloniphe futhi ngiphakamise uMthethosisekelo kanye nayo yonke eminye imithetho yaseRiphabhuliki, 
Imithetho eshiwo kwiSheduli 7 isusiwe, kodwa loku kulawulwa yisigaba 243 kanye noSheduli 6. 
Ukusetshenziswa 
Umthetho wamazwe ngamazwe osuyisiko ngumthetho kwiRephabhliki ngaphandle uma ungahambisani noMthethosisekelo noma umthetho wePhalamende. 
IRephabhliki ibophelelwa yizivumelwano zamazwengamazwe ezazibophelela iRephabhliki ngesikhathi soMthethosisekelo uqala ukusebenza. 
futhi ukwenza imisebenzi yesikhundla sami ngokwethembeka nangawo wonke amandla enginawo. 
Ukususwa kwemithetho 
Umthetho wamazwe ngamazwe osuyisiko 
Mina, A B

ukuba ngumeluleki weqiniso nowethembekile;

ngokuhlonipheka nangesithunzi; 
Afrika, futhi ngizothobela ngilandele, ngiphakamise futhi ngigcine uMthethosiseklo kanye nayo yonke eminye imithetho yaseRiphabhuliki; 
futhi umthetho owawusetshenziswa ngesikhathi umthethosisekelo uqala futhi owawubhekelwe nguhulumeni wesifundazwe.

Ukuze kujuliswe isiko lenqubo yentando yeningi elimiswe ngumthethosisekelo, iPhalamende kufanele lamukele imiqulu yamalungelo ehambisana noMthethosisekelo. 
Inqubo yokhetho 
noma yimuphi umnyango kahulumeni wokuphatha kukazwelonke, kwesifundazwe noma uhulumeni wendawo; 
Isifungo noma isiqinisekiso samalungu oMkhandlu kaZwelonke, izithunywa ezimile zesiGungu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe kanye namalungu esishayamthetho zezifundazwe 
futhi ngizokwabela ubulungiswa kubo bonke abantu ngokufana ngaphandle kokwesaba, kokuvuna noma ukukhinyabeza ngokulandela uMthethosisekelo kanye nomthetho. 
Isifungo noma isiqinisekiso soNgqongqoshe kanye namasekela oNgqongqoshe 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke uhlangana ukuze ukhethe uMongameli, noma uSomlomo noma iSekela likaSomlomo loMkhandlu; 
izingxenye zombuso kusho  
kufanele kubanjwe omunye umhlangano phakathi kwezinsuku eziyisikhombisa, ngesikhathi esishiwo ngumuntu owengamele. 
Ukwenziwa kwemisebenzi ngokukhuthala 
kodwa isimiso sesivumelwano esizisebenzayo ngokwaso futhi esamukelwe yiPhalamende sibangumthetho eRephabhliki ngaphandle uma siphambene noMthethosisekelo noma umthetho wePhalamende. 
esishiwo esimemezelweni sisuswa kusukela ngelanga elifanayo. 
Uma kungekho othola iningi lamavoti, lowo othole amavoti amancane kunabobonke kufanele achithwe okhethweni bese kuvotwa futhi kuvotelwa labo abasele njengoba kushiwo ku 6 ngenhla. 
Omele ukhetho eyedwa 
ingadlulisa amandla noma okwenza noma yimuphi umsebenzi okufanele wenziwe ngokusho komthetho, kwenye ingxenye kahulumeni ehlangene nokuphatha; 
noma isebenzise amandla noma yenze imisebenzi yenzela enye ingxenye kahulumeni ehlangene nokuphatha njengomele leyongxenye kahulumeni noma ngokuthatha amandla ayo. 
Umthetho wohlelo oludala ohambisana nokushiwo kwisigatshana ngenhla,  
Imitheshwana nezinqumo zoMkhandlu kaZwelonke ezisebenzayo ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, uyaqhubeka nokusebenza, kodwa kunakekelwe ushintsho olwenziwe noma loko okususiwe. 
ePhalamende, uMkhandlu kaZwelonke noma uMkhandlu weziGele kufanele uthathwe ngokuthi usho iPhalamende, uMkhandlu kaZwelonke noma uMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha; 
kufanele kuqhutshekwe nawo njengokusho koMthethosisekelo omusha. 
kufanele ithathwe ngokuthi ikhuluma ngoMongameli, iSekela likaMongameli, uNgqongqoshe, iSekela likaNgqongqoshe noma iKhabhinethi ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha njengoba kushiwo ku 9 wale Sheduli; 
kufanele kuthathwe ngokuthi kukhulunywa ngesishayamthetho sesifundazwe, uNdunankulu, uMkhandlu sokuphatha noma ilungu loMkhandlu sokuphatha ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha, njengoba sokuphathwa ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha, njengoba kushiwo ku 12, waleSheduli; 
kuMongameli woMkandlu wezigele, kufanele kuthathwe ngokuthi kukhulunywa ngosihlalo woMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe;

Isheduli 6 
Ukuqhubeka kwemithetho esikhona 
Isigaba 47 soMthethosisekelo omusha siyalengiswa kuze kube wukhetho lwesibili loMkhandlu kaZwelonke ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha. 
uMthethosisekelo omusha kusho uMthethosisekelo weRiphabhuliki yaseNingizimu Afrika, 1996; 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke 
awusebenzi kabanzi ngokwendawo nangayiphi enye indlela kunangesikhathi esingaphambi kokuthi uMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona uqale ukusebenza ngaphandle uma ushintshiwe ukuze usebenze kabanzi; 
Wonke umthetho owawusebenza uma uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza uyaqhubeka nokusebenza kodwa kuya ngokuthi  
futhi uphatha isikhundla njengelungu noma umphathi sikhundla njengoba kushiwo nguMthethosisekelo omusha. 
ngePhalamende ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha, uma ukuphathwa kwalowo mthetho kwabelwe noma kunikezelwe njengokusho koMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona noma leSheduli kuMkhandlu sokuphatha sikazwelonke; 
Noma yimuphi umsebenzi ongaphelile phambi komkhandlu weziGele uma uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza kufanele uyiswe kuMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe, futhi uMkhandlu kufanele siqhubeke nalowo msebenzi ngokusho koMthethosisekelo omusha. 
ngesishayamthetho sesifundazwe, uNdunankulu, uMkhandlu noma ilungu loMkhandlu esiphethe lesifundazwe 
imithetho yohlelo oludala kusho imithetho eyashaywa ngaphambi kokuba uMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalo uqale ukusebenza; 
futhi uyahambisana yini noMthethosisekelo omusha. 
noma ngolimi noma izilimi ezisemthethweni, kufanele kuthathwe ngokuthi kukhulunywa nganoma yiluphi ulimi olusemthethweni ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke njengoba wakhiwe ngokusho kuka, ngenhla, kufanele uthathwe ngokuthi ukhethwe ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha ukhethelwa isikhathi esiphela ngomhlaka 30 Epreli 1999. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke wakhiwe ngamalungu angu-400 esikhathini esiphela ngo 30 Epreli 1999, kodwa lokhu kulawulwa okushiwo kwisigaba 49 soMthethosisekelo omusha. 
eRephabhliki yaseNingizimu Afrika noma isabelo , kufanele uthathwe ngokuthi ukhuluma ngeRephabhliki yaseNingizimu Afrika ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha; 
ePhalamende, ngeNdlu yePhalamende noma umkhandlu wokushaya imithetho, noma isakhiwo seRephabhliki noma sesabelo, kufanele kuthathwe ngokuthi kukhulunwa

futhi Uyaqhubeka nokuphethwa yileso siphathimandla esasiwuphethe ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza ngendlela eshiwo nguMthethosisekelo omusha. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe 
Ngaphandle uma kungahambisani nokuhlosiwe noma kungafanele ngokucacileyo, uma umthetho wohlelo lwakudala  
Amalungiselelo esikhashana 
Noma yimuphi umuntu owayeyilungu loMkhandlu kaZwelonke uma uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, uba yilungu noma isiphathi sikhundla soMkhandlu kaZwelonke ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha, 
Umsebenzi ongaqedwanga ophambi kwePhalamende 
noma isishayamthetho sesifundazwe, uma ukuphathwa kwalowo mthetho kwabelwe noma kunikezelwe, njengokusho koMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona noma kwale Sheduli kuMkhandlu sokuphatha sesifundazwe; 
noma kuMongameli weZwe, uNgqongqoshe oMkhulu, uMphathi noma omunye umphathi omkhulu, iKhabhinethi, uMkhandlu soNgqongqoshe noma uMkhandlu sokuphatha seRephabhliki noma sesabelo, kufanele kuthathwe ngokuthi kukhulunywa  
isabelo kusho indawo yeRiphabhuliki eyayithathwa njengendawo ezimele noma ezibusayo ngomthetho waseNingizimu Afrika ngaphambi kokuthi uMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona uqale ukusebenza; 
uNdunankulu wesifundazwe ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha, uma ukuphathwa kwalowo mthetho kwabelwe noma kunikezelwe ngokusho koMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona noma leSheduli esigungwini sokuphatha sesifundazwe. 
Ngaphandle uma kungahambisani nalokho okuqonde ukushiwo noma ngokucacile kungafanele, uma umthetho owawukhona ngaphambi kokuthi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqale ukusebenza  
ngoMongameli ngaphansi komthethosisekelo omusha, uma ukuphathwa kwalo mthetho kwabelwe noma kunikezelwe ngokusho koMthethosisekelo ongaphambi kwalona noma kwale Sheduli esigungwini sokuphatha kaZwelonke; 
emva kokuthathwa kwesinqumo sokungamethembi uMongameli njengokwesigaba 102 soMthethosisekelo omusha.

Uhwebo lwasemigwaqeni 
kufanele isetshenziswe mayelana nemisebenzi yoMkhandlu kaZwelonke kangangoba ingasetshenziswa kunakekelwe lokho okushintshiwe nokususiwe. 
futhi ingaphakamisa abanye abantu njengezithunywa esingasuswa kuphela uma kungekho noma lingenele inani lababengamalungu omkhandlu wezigele angabakhona ukuze asebenze njengezithunywa ezimile. 
Iholo, izibonelelo, kanye nezinzuzo zowayeyilungu lendlu yezigele oqokelwe esikhundleni sokuba yisithunywa esimile noma njengelungu lesishayamthetho sesifundazwe alingeke lincishiswe ngenxa nje yokuthatha leso sikhundla. 
Isishayamthetho sesifundazwe njengokusho kuka ngenhla, kufanele sithathwe ngokuthi sakhethwa ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha sikhethelwa isikhathi esiphela ngomhlaka 30 Epreli 1999. 
aqhubeke njengoNgqongqoshe oshiwo esigabeni 91 soMthethosisekelo omusha, njengoba leso sigaba sibhaliwe kwisiJobelelo B. 
isishayamthetho sakhiwa yinani lamalungu elinqunyelwe leso sishayamthetho ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo owendulela lona kanye nenani lababengamalungu endlu yezigele ababangamalungu esishayamthetho njengokusho kuka 8 wale Sheduli. 
Kuze kube ngukuphela kwesikhathi sesishayamthetho wesifundazwe ngomhlaka 30 Epreli 1999, kodwa kunakekelwe okushiwo esigabeni 108, 
Kuze kube ngumhlaka 30 Epreli 1999, izigatshana 84, 89, 90, 91, 93, no 96 zoMthethosisekelo omusha kufanele zifundwe sengathi zibhalwe njengesiJobelelo B sale Sheduli. 
Izishayamthetho zezifundazwe 
unelungelo lokuba yilungu eliphelele elingavota lesishayamthetho sesifundazwe leso ayephakanyiswe kuso njengelunga loMkhandlu wezigele njengokusho kwesigaba 48 somthethosisekelo omdala. 
Iqembu elimelwe kwisishayamthetho sesifundazwe  
kufanele liphakamise izithunywa zalo esingasuswa phakathi kwabantu ababengamalungu omkhandlu wezigele uma uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza futhi abangabakhona ukuze basebenze njengezithunywa ezimile; 
Owayeyilungu lomkhandlu wezigele ongaqokelwanga esikhundleni sesithunywa esimile sesiGungu kaZwelonke sesifundazwe 
U, ngenhla, akamuvimbeli uNgqongqoshe owayeyilungu lendlu yezigele ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, ekubeni 
Isigaba 62 soMthethosisekelo omusha asisebenzi ekuphakamisweni nasekuqokelweni esikhundleni kwababengamalungu omkhandlu wezigele, njengezithunywa esingasuswa njengokusho kwalesi simiso. 
Isishayamthetho sesifundazwe kufanele siqokele esikhundleni izithunywa zaso esingasuswa ngokuhambisana neziphakamiso zamaqembu. 
Ababengamalungu omkhandlu wezigele 
Uma owayeyilungu lomkhandlu wezigele ekhetha ukungabi yilungu lesishayamthetho sesifundazwe lowo muntu uthathwa ngokuthi usishiye isikhundla sokubayilungu lomkhandlu weziGele ngelanga elandulela ilanga uMthethosisekelo omusha oqale ngalo ukusebenza. 
Imitheshwana nezibopho zesishayamthetho sesifundazwe ebezisebenza ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza ziyaqhubeka nokusebenza, kodwa kunakekelwe lokho okushintshiwe nokususiwe. 
U no, ngenhla, basebenza kuphela ekuqokweni kokuqala kwezithunywa zesiGungu kaZwelonke. 
Izithunywa Ezimile 
uba yilungu noma umphathi sikhundla wesishayamthetho saleso sifundazwe ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha kanye nanoma yimuphi umthethosisekelo wesifundazwe ongabakhona. 
Noma ngubani owayeyilungu noma ebambe isikhundla sesishayamthetho sesifundazwe ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, 
Imithethwana nezinqumo zomkhandlu wezigele obusebenza ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, 
Noma yimuphi umuntu owayenguMongameli, iSekela likaMongameli, uNgqongqoshe noma iSekela likaNgqongqoshe ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo owendulela lona, ngesikhathi uMthethosisekelo omusha uqala ukusebenza, 
uyaqhubeka kuleso sikhundla njengoba kusho uMthethosisekelo omusha, kodwa ngokulandela okushiwo ku, ngenhla. 
Ukhetho lwezishayamthetho zezifundazwe 
eziya noma ezivela kwisigungu sokuphatha sikazwelonke noma sesifundazwe noma kumnyango kahulumeni, umsebenzi kahulumeni, izikhungo zokuphepha noma yisiphi esinye isakhiwo. 
kubandakanya noma yiluphi ushintsho, inguquko noma ukususwa kanye nokushaywa kabusha kwanoma yimuphi umthetho kanye nanoma yisiphi esinye isinyathelo esithathwe ngaphansi kwalesi sigaba, kuthathwa ngokuthi kwenziwe ngaphansi kwalesi sigaba. 
okhethweni lokuqala lesishayamthetho sesifundazwe ngaphansi soMthethosisekelo omusha;

futhi ekugcwaliseni izikhala kwisishayamthetho, kanye nokugcwalisa, ukubheka kabusha, nokusetshenziswa kwezinhla zamaqembu ukuze kugcwaliswe izikhala, kuze kube yisikhathi sokhetho lwesibili lwesishayamthetho ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha. 
sihlala sinamandla okwengamela lowo mthetho uze unikezelwe kwisiphathimandla esiphakathi kwesigungu sokuphatha sesifundazwe ngokubeka kuka wale Sheduli.

noma ilungelo noma isibonelelo esitholwe noma isibopho noma isikweletu esakhiwe ngaphambi kokuba siphelelwe isikhathi. 
angashintsha noma aguqule umthetho ukuze alawule ukuhumushwa noma ukusebenza kwawo;

Mthethosisekelo, njengoba ushintshwe yisiJobelelo A saleyo Sheduli, iyasebenza  
Ikhophi ngesimemezelo ngasinye esikhishwe njengokubeka kuka noma , ngenhla, kufanele inikezwe uMkhandlu kaZwelonke kanye noMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe phakathi kwezinsuku ezingu-10 kushicilelwe isimemezelo. 
Aze athathe isikhundla ngaphansi koMthethosisekelo omusha uNdunankulu okhethwe emva kokhetho lokuqala lwesifundazwe, noma isifundazwe size sizishayele umthethosisekelo wesifundazwe, lokho okwenzeka kuqala kunokunye, 
futhi umuntu ophethe isikhundla njengomehluleli wenkantolo uyaqhubeka esiphethe leso sikhundla njengoba kusho umthetho osebenzayo kuleso sikhundla, kube kunakekelwe  
noma angalawula noma yiluphi olunye udaba okunesidingo sokuthi lulawulwe ngenxa yaloku kunikezela, kubandakanya ukudluliswa noma ukwetshelekisa ngabasebenzi, noma ukwedluliselwa kwempahla, izikweletu, amalungelo, kanye nezibopho 
U, ngenhla akasebenzi emva kweminyaka emibili uMthethosisekelo omusha waqala ukusebenza.

omusha uqala ukusebenza, ziyaqhubeka nokusebenza nokuba namandla eziwanikwa yimithetho ezithintayo, 
kwisiphathimandla esiphakathi kwesifundazwe esiqokwe uMkhandlu sokuphatha sesifundazwe.

banegunya lokunikwa isikhundla esisodwa noma ngaphezulu kuMkhandlu esikhulu ngokulingana nenani lezihlalo zenhlangano kwisishayamthetho 
noma ukuklomelisa kwesikhathi esimisiwe noma isimo sokusebenza noma ezinye izinzuzo, okwenzeka phakathi komhlaka 27 Apreli 1993 no 30 Septemba 1994 
kuzothi emva kokuqala ukusebenza komthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika wango 1996, ziqhubeke, zinombono wokwakha  
Izikhundla zeKhabhinethe kufanele zabelwe iqembu ngalinye elibambe iqhaza ngokulandela uhlelo lokubala olulandelayo: 
uma kubanesidingo ngezizathu zoMthethosisekelo noma ngenxa yokubusa kahle kukahulumeni, ashintshe noma yisiphi isinqumo ngaphansi kwesigaba, ngaphandle kokushiwo esigatshaneni ; 
aqoke maqondana naleso sikhundla ngasinye ilungu lo Mkhandlu kaZwelonke eliyilungu leqembu elabelwe leso sikhundla ngaphansi kwesigaba, njengoNgqongqoshe obhekelele leso sikhundla; 
ISekela lika Mongameli lingasebenzisa amandla futhi lenze imisebenze abekelwe isikhundla seSekela likaMongameli nguMthethosisekelo noma abelwe leso sikhundla nguMongameli. 
Isigaba 93 soMthethosisekelo omusha sithathwa ngokuthi sifundeka ngalendlela elandelayo: 
Umbutho Wezokuvikela KaZwelonke uzoba namandla futhi uzokwenza umsebenzi wawo ngokwenza lokho okuzozuza umphakathi kaZwelonke kuphela ngokumaqondana nesahluko 11 somthetho-sisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika, 1996. 
Amalungu oMkhandlu eSikhulu ayazibikela ilungu ngalinye kuNdunankulu nakuSishayamthetho sesiFundazwe ngokuphathwa kwezikhundla zawo, 
Inani lezikhundla ezizokwabelwa iqembu elibamba iqhaza ngalinye linqunywa ngokwehlukanisa inani eliphelele lezihlalo zaleloqembu kuMkhandlu kaZwelonke ngesabelo esishiwo kwisigaba . 
lelo Sekela likaNgqongqoshe kufanele ngegama lalowo Ngqongqoshe, lisebenzise futhi lenze noma yimaphi amandla noma imisebenzi eyabelwe lowo Ngqongqoshe 
Ikhomishani ingaguqula noma ichibiyele isivumelwano, ukuqashwa, ukukhushulelwa esikhundleni esiphakeme noma umklomelo uma kungalungile noma kwamukelekile esimweni salolo daba; 
ISekela likaMongameli liba sesikhundleni  
ngokusho konthetho noma yimuphi noma ngenye indlela uNgqongqoshe angabela ngayo iSekela likaNgqongqoshe ngokuhambisana nemiyalelo kaMongameli; 
Izichibiyelo kwizigaba zomthethosisekelo owedlule 
kufanele afinyelele esinqunyweni nganoma yikuphi ukuqoka okungaphansi kwesigaba uma kubanesidingo ngezizathu zoMthethosisekelo noma zokubusa kahle kukahulumeni. 
ukufaka esikhundleni sepharagrafu sesigatshana ipharagrafu elandelayo: 
ukufaka esikhundleni sepharagrafu sesigatshana ipharagrafu elandelandelayo: 
ukuphenya kanye nokuvimbela ubugebengu obuhleliwe noma ubugebengu obudinga uphenyo kanye nokuvimbela ubugebengu kukaZwelonke noma amakhono aphezulu; 
Uma ilungu elithintekile lehluleka ukuhambisana nesidingo sikaNdunankulu esibekwe ngaphansi kwesigatshana, uNdunankulu angalisusa lelo lungu ehhovisi emva kokuxoxisana nalo, 
uma lingekho iqembu elinezihlalo ezingu 80 noma ezingaphezulu eMkhandlwini, iqembu elinezihlalo eziningi kunawo wonke 
anqume ngezikhundla ezizokwabelwa iqembu elibamba iqhaza ngalinye ngokulandela inani lezikhundla eza belwe amaqembu ngokusho kwesigatshana ; 
Umphumela, ngaphandle kokushiwo kwingaba, ukhomba inani lezikhundla okufanele zabelwe leloqembu. 
ukusebenzisa amandla ashiwo kusiqephu, noma sesigatshana esithinta umuntu ongelona ilungu lenhlangano kaNdunankulu, 
Uma uNgqongqoshe ehluleka ukuphatha isikhundla ngokuhambisana nomgomo weKhabhinethe, uMongameli angafuna ukuthi uNgqongqoshe othintekile aqondise ukuphathwa kwaleso sikhundla ukuze kuhambisane nalowo mgomo. 
IsiGungu esikhulu sesifundazwe 
noma engeyena umholi weqembu elibamba iqhaza, futhi emuva kokubonisana nomholi weqembu lalowo Ngqongqoshe; 
njengelungu loMkhandlu eSikhulu eliqokelwe leso sikhundla; 
ukusebenzisa amandla ashiwo kusiqephu, noma saleso sigatshana isinqumo sikaNdunankulu singumnqamulajuqu; 
isinqumo somholi weqembu lowo muntu ayilungu lalo siyabusa, 
Umphumela, kunganakwa izingxenye kusukela enombolweni yesithathu nezilandelayo, uma zikhona izabelo zezihlalo zesikhundla ngasinye. 
Isabelo sezihlalo esiqondene nesikhundla ngasinye kufanele sibalwe ngokwehlukanisa inani eliphelele lezihlalo kuMkhandlu kaZwelonke 
UNdunankulu Wesifundazwe kufanele, emva kokuxhumana nabaholi bezinhlangano ezibamba iqhaza, enze lokhu  
futhi uMongameli kanye nabanye abawusebenzelayo abathintekile, kufanele uma bephoqelela leso sigatshana bazame ukuthola ukuvumelana: 
uma kunguNgqongqoshe oshiwo esigabeni 91, emuva kokubonisana namasekela kaMongameli nabaholi bamaqembu abamba iqhaza. 
futhi ngokususa amagama athi, lo Mthetho-sisekelo, noma yikuphi lapho kuvela khona kwisigaba 236, kufakwe ukuthi, Umthetho-sisekelo omusha. 
noNgqongqoshe abangeqile ku 27 abangamalungu oMkhandlu kaZwelonke futhi beqokwe njengokusho kwezigatshana kuya ku ; 
Amalungu oMkhandlu eSikhulu kufanele engamele izikhundla zawo ngokumayelana nenqubo ekhishwe uMkhandlu. 
elibanjwe yiwowonke amaqembu abambe iqhaza ngenani lezikhundla ezizoqokelwa oNgqongqoshe abashiwo esigatshaneni bese kuhlanganiswa noyedwa. 
noma omunye umuntu noma yimuphi ukuba abambe isikhundla saleloSekela likaNgqongqoshe sonke, ngokujwayelekile noma maqondana nokusetshenziswa noma ukwenziwa kwanoma yimaphi amandla noma imisebenzi ebaluliwe. 
Isigaba 96 soMthethosisekelo omusha sithathwa ngokuthi siqukethe lezi zigatshana ezilandelayo ezinezezelwe: 
kanye noNgqongqoshe ongeqile koyedwa ongelona ilungu loMkhandlu ka Zwelonke oqokwe njengokusho kwesigatshana, kodwa nguMongameli, 
linelungelo lokwabelwa isikhundla esisodwa noma ngaphezulu seKhabhinethe, esiqokelwa oNgqongqoshe abashiwo kwisigatshana,

Ukuchibiyelwa kwesigaba 236 kumthetho-sisekelo owedlule  
Izikhundla kwiSigungu Esikhulu kumele zabiwe kwizinhlangano ezibambe iqhaza njengoba kushiwo esigabeni 91, futhi uma kusetshenziswa lowo mthetho oshiwo kuleso sigaba:  
Ukuchibiyelwa kwesigaba 227 kumthetho-sisekelo owedlule ngokufaka isigatshana esilandelayo esikhundleni sesigatshana : 
Iqembu linelungelo lokwabelwa isikhundla esisodwa noma ezingaphezulu zobusekela bukangqongqoshe ngamanani alinganayo kanye nangendlela efana naleyo esentshenziselwe ukwabiwa.kwezikhundla zeKhabhinethe. 
Uhulumeni, umnyango kahulumeni, ukuphathwa kukahulumeni noma eZokuphepha okwathi masinyane ngaphambi kokuqaliswa komthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika, ngo 1996 , 
ukuqokwa koKhomishani beZifundazwe; 
futhi kulokho kusetshenziswa uma kuleso sigaba kukhulunywa ngoNgqongqoshe noma isikhundla sikaNgqongqoshe noma isikhundla seSekela likaNgqonqoshe, ngokuqondana. 
UMongameli angaqoka ikhomishani ezobuka kabusha isiphetho noma isichibiyelo sesivumelwano, ukuqashwa noma ukukhushulelwa esikhundleni esiphakeme, 
zizokwehlela phezu Kombutho Wezokuvikela kaZwelonke ngokumayelana nokulawulwa nguNgqongqoshe weZokuvikela. 
Ngokumayelana nezinkomba zikaNgqongqoshe WezoKuphepha nokuVikela, uKhomishani kaZwelonke uzoba nalo mthwalo ; 
futhi noma yimuphi umthetho okhuluma ngalowo Ngqongqoshe kufanele uhunyushwe ngokuthi ubandakanye iSekela lika Ngqongqoshe elibambe ngokusho kwesabelo ngaphansi kwesigaba sikaNgqongqoshe obanjelwe yilelo Sekela likaNgqongqoshe. 
ukusetshenziswa kwamandla ashiwo kwisigaba, noma kuleso sigatshana athinta umuntu ongesilo ilungu leqembu likaMongameli, 
Lapho lesi sigaba sidinga ukuba umuntu aziswe okuthile, lolo lwazi kufanele lowo muntu alunikwe ngolimi aluqonda kahle. 
futhi lokusungula nokujoyina imifelandawonye.

futhi isidingo sokulungisa imiphumela yemithetho nenqubo eyedlule eyayibandlulula ngokobuzwe.

Wonke umuntu unelungelo  
Wonke umuntu unelungelo lokuthi noma yiyiphi ingxabano engaxazululwa ngokusebenzisa umthetho, inqunywe yinkantolo yomthetho ecaleni eligculisayo elivulekele umphakathi noma, 
futhi lokuxoxisana ngokuhlanganyela; 
lokusungula nokujoyina izinhlangano zabaqashi; 
lokuvikelwa ekuphathweni ngendlela engafanele, ekubeni anganakekelwa, ekuhlukunyezweni nasekuphathweni ngendlela eyehlisa isithunzi; 
futhi lokuba kuvikelwe imvelo, ukuze kusizakale izizukulwana zamanje nezizayo, ngemithetho efanele nangezinye izinyathelo ezimisiwe okuqondwe ngazo  
Akukho okushiwo kulesisigaba okungavimba umbuso ekubeni uthathe izinyathelo zokushaya imithetho nezinye izinyathelo ngenhloso yokuphumelelisa uguquko kwezomhlaba, amanzi nokunye okuyelene nalokho, 
ezingabandlululi ngokohlanga; 
Imiphakathi enamasiko, izinkolo kanye nezilimi ezithile 
lokuba icala lakhe lethanyelwe ngumphakathi enkantolo ejwayelekile yamacala;

futhi nanoma yiluphi ulwazi olusezandleni zomunye umuntu oludingekayo ekusetshenzisweni noma ekuvikelweni kwanoma yimaphi amalungelo. 
futhi ezigcina amazinga angekho ngaphansi kwamazinga asezikoleni ezingaqhathaniswa nezixhaswa yizimali zombuso. 
uhlinzekele ukuhlaziywa kabusha kwaleso sinyathelo enkantolo noma, esimweni esilungile kuhlaziye inkundla ezimele nengavuni cala;

Wonke umntwana unelungelo  
futhi lokuphathwa ngendlela futhi aboshwe ezimweni ezikhombisa ukubonelela iminyaka yakhe; 
ukuthokozela amasiko abo, ukuqhuba inkolo yabo nokusebenzisa ulimi lwabo; 
inani lezimali ezatshalwa umbuso nemali umbuso owasiza ngayo, ekutholakaleni kwaleyo mpahla nasekuyithuthukiseni ukuze ibeyinzuzo; 
kodwa akekho ovunyelwe ukusebenzisa lawa malungelo ngendlela engahambisani nanoma yisiphi isimiso soMqulu wamaLungelo. 
Ubudlelwane phakathi kwabasebenzi nabaqashi 
lokungahlanganiswa nabanye abantu ababoshiwe abaneminyaka yobudala engaphezulu kuka 18; 
ukuthi kungenzeka yini; 
Akekho umuntu ongalelwa ukuba athole usizo lwezokwelashwa oluphuthumayo. 
lokungaboshwa ngaphandle uma ukuboshwa kwakhe kuyisinyathelo sokugcina esingathathwa, okuyothi uma kwenzeka, ngaphezulu kwamalungelo anikwe umntwana esigabeni kanye no 35 
futhi isizathu sokuthathwa kwempahla. 
Yilowo nalowo muntu unelungelo  
Esimweni lapho umthetho unganciphisa ilungelo kulesi sahluko, ukuncishiswa kwelungelo makuhambisane nesigaba 36 . 
ukuze ulungise imiphumela yobandlululo ngobuzwe lwesikhathi esedlule, kodwa konke okuqhelile ezimisweni zalesisigaba kufanele kuhambisane nezimiso zesigaba 36. 
futhi ukhuthaze ukuthi kubenombuso osebenza ngokukhuthala. 
Ukuvumeleka ukuya eNkantolo 
Bonke abasebenzi banelungelo  
Ubufakazi obutholakale ngendlela ephambene nanoma yiliphi ilungelo elikuMqulu wamaLungelo kufanele bungangeniswa njengobufakazi ecaleni uma ukungeniswa kwalobo bufakazi bungenza ukuthi icala lingagculisi noma kungakhinyabeza ukuphathwa kobulungiswa. 
lokuphikisa ukubasemthethweni kokuvalelwa kwakhe mathupha phambi kwenkantolo, futhi uma kutholakala ukuthi loko kuvalelwa akukho emthethweni adedelwe; 
Umuntu noma umphakathi owathathelwa impahla emva kuka 19 June 1913, ngenxa yemithetho noma izenzo unelungelo 
ongamfanele umuntu oneminyaka yobudala elingana neyalowo mntwana; 
Akekho umuntu ongephucwa impahla ngaphandle uma kumiswe umthetho osebenza ngokufanayo kubobonke abantu, futhi awukho umthetho ongavumela ukuthi umuntu aphucwe impahla engazange anikezwe ithuba lokuziphendulela. 
lokusungula nokujoyina izinhlangano zabasebenzi; 
futhi udokotela oqokwe nguye. 
Wonke umuntu unelungelo lokukwazi ukuthola indlu efanelekile. 
Impahla ingathathwa kuphela njengoba kubekwe wumthetho osebenza kubobonke abantu ngokufanayo  
lokuzibandakanya ezenzweni nasezinhlelweni zezinhlangano zabasebenzi; 
futhi uma kuzoba nesinxephezelo inani, isikhathi nendlela yokusikhokha isinxephezelo okuvunyelwane ngaso noma kunqunywe noma kwamukelwe yinkantolo. 
noma ekupheleni kosuku lokuqala lwenkantolo emva kwesikathi esingamahora angu-48 sesidlulile ngaphandle kwesikhathi esejwayelekile sokusebenza kwenkantolo, noma nosuku olungelona lokusebenza kwenkantolo; 
lokuvikelwa ezimweni zokuxhashazwa emsebenzini; 
Umbuso kumele uthathe izinyathelo zomthetho nezinye izinyathelo, ezilungile, ngokusemandleni awo, ukweseka isimo esizokwenza izakhamuzi zikwazi ukuthola umhlaba ngendlela egculisayo. 
Umbuso kufuneka wenze amalungelo asesigatshaneni asebenze ngokushaya umthetho kazwelonke futhi lomthetho ungahlinzekela izinyathelo ezifanele ezinganciphisa umsebenzi wokwengamela izidingo zalelilungelo kanye nezindleko kumbuso. 
Umbuso kufanele uthathe izinyathelo zomthetho ezifanele nezinye izinyathelo, ngokusemandleni ombuso ukwenza ukuba ukuphumelela kwaleli lungelo kuqhubekele phambili. 
futhi bakhe, bajoyine futhi bagcine izinhlangano zamasiko, zenkolo nezezilimi kanye nezinye izinhlangano zomphakathi. 
umlando wobunikazi bempahla nokusetshenziswa kwayo; 
lokwaziswa ngokushesha ngezizathu zokuvalelwa kwakhe; 
lokuba angaphoqwa ukuhlambuluka noma ukuvuma izinto ezingase zisetshenziswe njengobufakazi ecaleni lakhe; 
Isigatshana asizivimbeli izimali zombuso ezixhasa izakhiwo zemfundo ezizimele. 
Zonke izinhlangano zabasebenzi nezinhlangano zabaqashi zine nelungelo  
futhi lokuzibandakanya ezenzweni nasezinhlelweni zezinhlangano zabaqashi; 
Ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuthi leli lungelo kuyafinyelelwa kulona ngempela, nokuphoqelelwa kwaleli lungelo, umbuso kufanele uhlolisise yonke imigudu efanele yemfundo, kubandakanya nezakhiwo zemfundo ezifundisa ngolimi olulodwa, kube kunakekelwe okulandelayo  
lokunakekelwa kwezempilo, okubandakanya ukunakekelwa kwezempilo okuqondene nokubeletha; 
Inani, isikhathi nendlela yokunxephezela kufanele kube elinganayo negculisayo, 
Umthetho kazwelonke ungamiswa ukulawula isivumelwano esihlanganyelwe. 
futhi lokufaka isicelo sokudlulisa icala noma ukuhlaziywa kwalo yinkantolo enkulu. 
Zonke izinyunyane zabasebenzi, izinhlangano zabaqashi kanye nomqashi zinelungelo lokuvumelana ngokuhlanganyela. 
lokuba icala liqulwe ngolimi aluzwayo, noma uma loko kungaphumeleli ukuqulwa kwecala kutolikelwe kulolo limi alwaziyo; 
Umthetho kazwelonke ungagunyaza ukuhlelelwa ezokuphepha enyunyanini okungavunyelwana ngakho ngokuhlanganyela. 
ukukhuthaza ukulondolozwa kwemvelo; 
inzuzo yomphakathi ibandakanya ukuzibophezela kwesizwe ekuthini kuguqulwe uhlelo lobunikazi bomhlaba, nasekuthini; 
Wonke umuntu ovalelwe, kubandakanya noma yisiphi isiboshwa esidonsa isigwebo, unelungelo  
lokungaphoqwa ukuba anike ubufakazi obuzomethwesa ngecala; 
Yilowo nalowo muntu unelungelo lokuphathwa yiminyango nezakhiwo zombuso ngendlela esemthethweni, efanele futhi elandela inqubo egculisayo. 
ngendlela eshiwo ehlinzikelwe ngumthetho wePhalamende, lokuthola ilungelo elime laqina emthethweni noma lokunikezwa usizo olungafaniswa nokuqiniswa kwalelolungelo. 
Ukuthola Ulwazi 
inani engathengiswa ngalo ngaleso sikhathi; 
eveza ukulingana phakathi kwemali yomphakathi kanye nakulabo abathintekile, emva kokubhekela bonke abathintekile izimo ezibandakanya  
ukuvimbela ukunukubezeka nokucekelwa phansi kwempilo yezitshalo neyezilwane; 
lokunikezwa isigwebo esisinda kancane kunesinye esimisiwe uma isigwebo esimiselwe lelo cala sishintshiwe phakathi kwesikhathi sokwenziwa kwecala nesikhathi sokugwetshwa; 
ezibhaliswe nombuso; 
futhi ngomphumela wokungasho lutho; 
Kuzona zonke izinto ezithinta umntwana, kuyobekwa phambili izidingo zakhe. 
IPhalamende kufanele lishaye umthetho oshiwo kwizigatshana . 
futhi nokuqinisekisa intuthuko engapheli nokusetshenziswa ngendlela efanele kwemithombo yemvelo kube kugqugquzelelwa ukuthuthuka okufanele komnotho nendlela yokuphila yomphakathi. 
Esimweni lapho umthetho unganciphisa ilungelo kulesi sahluko, ukuncishiswa kwelungelo makuhambisane nesigaba 36. 
Yilowo nalowo muntu unelungelo lokuphathwa ngendlela efanele emsebenzini. 
Awukho umthetho oyovumela ukususwa abathintekayo benganikwanga ithuba lokuziphendulela. 
futhi lokukhululwa ekuvalelweni uma izidingo zobulungiswa zivuma, kodwa ngemibandela efanelekile. 
lokuthula angasho lutho; 
Umuntu noma umphakathi onelungelo lomhlaba elintengantengayo ngokomthetho ngenxa yomthetho noma izenzo zesikhathi esedlule ezibandlulula ngobuzwe, unelungelo 
Yilowo nalowo muntu onamalungelo athintwe yisinyathelo sokuphatha, unelungelo lokunikezwa izizathu ezibhaliwe zaleso sinyathelo. 
nanoma yiluphi ulwazi olusezandleni zombuso; 
amahora angu-48 emva kokuboshwa; 
lokuthola imfundo eyisisekelo, kuhlanganisa imfundo eyisisekelo yabantu abadala, ezikhungweni zombuso noma ezikhungweni ezithola usizo embusweni; 
lokuphila endaweni engesiyo ingozi empilweni noma kwinhlalakahle yakhe; 
Ulimi namasiko 
lokunakekelwa ngumndeni, noma ukunakekelwa ngabazali noma ukunakekelwa okunye okufanele uma lowo mntwana esusiwe emndenini; 
lokuba nommeli amnikezwa umbuso ngezindleko zombuso, emacaleni ombango athinta umntwana, uma ukunganikezwa ummeli kungaba nomphumela wokwehluleka kakhulu kobulungiswa; 
ekuveleni kokuqala phambi kwenkantolo emva kokuboshwa, lokuba adedelwe ngaphandle uma ethweswa icala futhi inkantolo inquma ukuthi aqhubeke evalelwe; 
futhi lenhlalakahle okubandakanya, usizo olufanele uma umuntu engakwazi ukuzondla nokondla labo okufanele abondle. 
noma obeka inhlalakahle engozini, imfundo, impilo yomzimba noma yengqondo, noma ukuthuthuka komoya, kwesimilo noma kobudlelwano nomphakathi, komntwana, esimweni esibucayi; 
umntwana angaboshwa kuphela isikhathi okuyisona esifushane angaboshwa ngaso, futhi unelungelo  
Akekho umuntu ongasuswa emzini wakhe noma kudilizwe indlu yakhe ngaphandle kwesinqumo senkantolo esenziwe ngemuva kokuba ibheke izimo ezithile ezifanelekile 
Yilowo nalowo muntu unelungelo lokusungula nokugcina,ngezindleko zakhe, izikhungo zemfundo zangasese  
lokuba avalelwe ngaphansi kwesimo esihlonipha isithunzi sobuntu, kubandakanye ukuthi okungenani ukulolonga umzimba nokuhlinzeka ngezindleko zombuso, indawo eyanele, umsoco owanele, izinto zokufunda ezanele kanye nokwelashwa kwempilo okwanele; 
njengoba kuhlinzekelwa ngumthetho wePhalamende lokubuyiselwa leyo mpahla, noma lokuthola usizo olufanele. 
anelungelo elilinganayo ngaphambi kwekomidi elihlanganyelwe lePhalamende kanye noMkhandlu njengoba benalo ngaphambi kwePhalamende noma uMkhandlu. 
inkantolo kufanele imdedele umuntu ngaphandle uma kudingekile ukuba aqhubeke evalelwe ukuze kubuyiselwe uxolo nokuthula; 
kanye nesigatshana esimayelana nabantwana abaneminyaka engu- 15 nabangaphansi. 
Ukwelulwa kokuqala kwesikhathi sesimo esibucayi kufanele kwenziwe ngesinqumo esivunjwe yiningi lamalungu oMkhandlu. 
nezinhlelo ezibekelwe leso sidingo, futhi kufanele isebenzise yonke eminye imigudu ekhona ngaphambi kokudlulisela udaba enkantolo ukuba ixazulule leyo ngxabano.

Isimo esibucayi 
ubunjalo nobungako bokunciphisa; 
kumise uhulumeni weRiphabhuliki wonkana onobuciko, osebenzela obala, ophendulayo futhi odidiyelwe kahle; 
IPhalamende lingagxambukela ngokwamukela umthetho, ngendlela ehambisana nesigaba 76, mayelana nodaba olufakwe ohlwini lukaSheduli 5, uma kunesidingo  
Ngaphandle uma kwenziwe ngendlela ehlinzekelwe kwisigatshana noma esinye sezimiso zoMthethosisekelo awukho umthetho onganciphisa noma yiliphi ilungelo elihlinzekelwe kuMqulu wamaLungelo. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke unganquma ukwelula isikhathi sokusebenza kwesimemezelo sesimo esibucayi ngesikhathi esingeqile ezinyangeni ezintathu. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke neisGungu sikaZwelonke weziFundazwe kufanele kokubili kumise ikomidi elihlangene lokushaya le mitheshwana elizomisa imitheshwana nezinqumo mayelana nomsebenzi odidiyelwe woMkhandlu neisGungu, kubandakanya imitheshwana nezinqumo  
Ukwenza loku ngokukhetha uMongameli, ngokuba yinkundla kazwelonke yokucwaningwa kwezindaba phambi komphakathi, ngokushaya imithetho kanye nokuhlolisisa nokuqapha izenzo zikahulumeni. 
yokumiswa kwezinqubo zokugqugquzela uhlelo lokushaya imithetho, kubandakanya ukubeka imikhawulo yesikhathi sokuqeda isinyathelo esithile ohlelweni; 
ubudlelwane phakathi kokunciphisa nezinjongo zawo; 
noma yimuphi umuntu owenza isicelo egameni lomunye umuntu ongakwazi ukuzenzela yena; 
futhi isikhathi esingeqile ezinsukwini ezingu 21 kusukela osukwini lwesimemezelo ngaphandle uma uMkhandlu kaZwelonke unquma ukwelula isikhathi sesimemezelo. 
sokugsima amazinga asemqoka kazwelonke sokumisa amazinga okungafanele ehliswe okunikela ngemisebenzi yombuso; 
kanye nenhlangano efaka isicelo ngenhloso yokuzuzela amalungu ayo.

Ukumenyezelwa kwesimo esibucayi, kanye nomthetho owenziwe noma isinyathelo noma yisiphi esithathwe kulandela leso simemezelo, kungasebenza kuphela  
futhi isimemezelo sesimo esibucayi sidingekile ukuze kubuyiselwe uxolo nokuthula. 
 ukuxolelwa kombuso, noma komuntu noma yimuphi mayelana nesenzo esingekho emthethweni; 
Umuntu ovalelwe kumele avunyelwe ukuqoka, kanye nokuvakashelwa ngudokotela noma ngasiphi isikhathi esifanele; 
Uma kuhunyushwa nanoma yimuphi umthetho, futhi uma kuthuthukiswa umthetho owejwayelekile noma umthetho wesintu, yileyo naleyo nkantolo, noma inkundla kumele ikhuthaze umoya, inhloso kanye nezinjongo zoMqulu wamaLungelo. 
Yonke imikhakha kahulumeni kufanele iqaphele futhi ilandele imigomo ebekwe kulesi sahluko futhi kumele yenze imisebenzi yayo ngokulandela uhlaka olunikezwa yilesi sahluko. 
uhlinzekele indlela efanele yokusebenza kanye nenqubo yokugqugquzela ukusonjululwa kwengxabano phakathi kohulumeni. 
UMkhandlu kaZwelonke kanye noMkhandlu kaZwelonke weziFundazwe babamba iqhaza ekushayweni kwemithetho ngendlela ebekwe kulo Mthethosisekelo. 
futhi yokulawula umsebenzi  
Indawo yokuhlala kwePhalamende ise Kapa, kodwa umthetho wePhalamende oshaywe ngendlela ehambisana nezigaba 76 no, unganquma ukuthi iPhalamende lihlala kwenye indawo. 
Umuntu ongadedelwanga njengokusho kwesibuyekezo esikwindima noma ongadedelwanga ngemuva kokubuyekezwa ngaphansi kwalesi sigaba 
emkhakheni kahulumeni wezifundazwe linikezwe isishayamthetho njengoba kushiwo esigabeni 104; 
Noma yinini lapho umuntu evalelwe ngaphandle kokuthethwa kwecala ngaphansi komthetho wesimo esibucayi izimiso ezilandelayo kufanele ziqikelelwe: 
futhi ngokugwema ukwethwesana ngamacala phambi komthetho. 
UMongameli angabizela iPhalamende emhlanganweni ongejwayelekile noma ngasiphi isikhathi ukuze lenze umsebenzi ongejwayelekile.

Mayelana nokubandlululwa okungamukelekile ngokohlanga, ibala, ubuzwe noma imvelaphi, ubulili, inkolo noma ulimi.

Ukuhunyushwa komqulu wamalungelo 
kusebenzise amandla ako futhi nokwenza nemisebenzi ngendlela yokungeyi amandla endawo, ukusebenza kanye nobuqotho bohulumeni beminye imikhakha; 
futhi okucwaninga, ngendlela eshiwo yisigaba 75, noma yimuphi omunye umthetho owamukelwe nguMkhandlu kaZwelonke.

Isahluko 4 
Amalungu eKhabhinethi, amalungu ePhalamende likazwelonke kanye namalungu amele uMkhandlu seziFundazwe sikazwelonke 
Umuntu ovalelwe unelungelo lokuvela qobo lwakhe phambi kwenkantolo, ukumelwa ngummeli kulolo daba futhi nokwethula izizathu eziphikisa ukuthi aqhubeke esekuvalelweni; 
yokumiswa kwamakomidi ahlangenyelwe akhiwe ngabamele imikhakha yomibili yePhalamende, uMkhandlu nesiGungu, ukuze acwaninge futhi wethule imibiko ngeMithethosivivinywa ehlongozwa ezigabeni 74 no 75 esidluliselwe kulawo makomiti; 
Yonke imikhakha kahulumeni nazo zonke izingxenye zombuso emkhakheni ngamunye kufanele  
ngokusizana nokwesekana; 
vumelana nezimiso zeRiphubliki ngaphansi komthetho womhlaba wonke omiselwe isimo esibucayi; 
impilo yezwe yesatshiswa ngenxa yempi, yokuhlaselwa, yokuvukelwa kombuso, yeziphithiphithi, yenhlekelele yemvelo noma yesehlakalo esibucayi emphakathini; 
kugcine uxolo, ubumbano lwesizwe, nokungahlukaniseki kweRiphabhuliki; 
wekomidi lokubuyekezwa komthethosisekelo;

Uhulumeni wobumbano 
Mayelana nobugqili nokwenziwa isigqila ukwenziwa isigqila nokusetshenziswa ngempoqo. 
Sikwenza loku ikakhulukazi ngokubamba iqhaza ekushayweni kwemithetho kazwelonke nokuba yinkundla kazwelonke yokucwaningwa kwezindaba ezithinta izifundazwe phambi komphakathi. 
umuntu omdala oyilungu lomndeni noma umngane walowo ovalelwe kufanele atshelwe ngokushesha okungase kwenzeka ngokuvalelwa kwalowo muntu. 
kodwa kungahlanganisi, ngaphandle kwendlela eshiwo yisigatsana , udaba olufakwe kuluhlu lukaSheduli 5; 
sokugcina ubumbano lomnotho; 
noma yimuphi umuntu ofaka isicelo njengelungu, noma owenza lokho egameni leqembu noma lomkhakha othile wabantu; 
noma sokuvimbela isenzo esingafanele esithathwa yisifundazwe esingakhinyabeza esinye isifundazwe noma izwe ngokuphelele. 
lesi saziso kumele sisho igama lomuntu nalapho evalelwe khona nesimo esibucayi aboshwe ngaphansi kwaso;
